string) http.HandlerFunc {\n501\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n502\t\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n503\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n504\t\t\t\treturn\n505\t\t\t}\n506\t\n507\t\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n508\t\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n509\t\t\tif _, err := rand.Read(newMEK); err != nil {\n510\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate new MEK: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n511\t\t\t\treturn\n512\t\t\t}\n513\t\n514\t\t\t// Call the admin API's rotate endpoint\n515\t\t\trotateURL := adminURL\n516\t\t\tif rotateURL == \"\" {\n517\t\t\t\trotateURL = \"http://127.0.0.1:9001/admin/key/rotate\"\n518\t\t\t}\n519\t\n520\t\t\t// Send the new MEK as hex-encoded string\n521\t\t\tmekHex := hex.EncodeToString(newMEK)\n522\t\t\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(r.Context(), http.MethodPost, rotateURL, strings.NewReader(mekHex))\n523\t\t\tif err != nil {\n524\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to create request: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n525\t\t\t\treturn\n526\t\t\t}\n527\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\")\n528\t\n529\t\t\tresp, err := adminClient.Do(req)\n530\t\t\tif err != nil {\n531\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to call admin API: %v\", err), http.StatusBadGateway)\n532\t\t\t\treturn\n533\t\t\t}\n534\t\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n535\t\n536\t\t\t// Copy response headers and body\n537\t\t\tfor k, v := range resp.Header {\n538\t\t\t\tw.Header()[k] = v\n539\t\t\t}\n540\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(resp.StatusCode)\n541\t\t\tio.Copy(w, resp.Body)\n542\t\t}\n543\t}\n544\t\n545\t// EncryptionStatsResponse holds encryption statistics for a bucket listing.\n546\ttype EncryptionStatsResponse struct {\n547\t\tEncryptedCount  int            `json:\"encrypted_count\"`\n548\t\tPlaintextCount  int            `json:\"plaintext_count\"`\n549\t\tTotalCount      int            `json:\"total_count\"`\n550\t\tEncryptedBytes  int64          `json:\"encrypted_bytes\"`\n551\t\tPlaintextBytes  int64          `json:\"plaintext_bytes\"`\n552\t\tKeyIDs          []string       `json:\"key_ids\"`\n553\t\tKeyUsage        map[string]int `json:\"key_usage\"`\n554\t\tCoveragePercent float64        `json:\"coverage_percent\"`\n555\t}\n556\t\n557\t// EncryptionStatsHandler returns encryption statistics for the bucket.\n558\tfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n559\t\treturn d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl()\n560\t}\n561\t\n562\t// EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth returns the encryption stats handler with authentication.\n563\tfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n564\t\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl())\n565\t}\n566\t\n567\tfunc (d *Dashboard) encryptionStatsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n568\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n569\t\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n570\t\n571\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n572\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n573\t\n574\t\t\t// Use no delimiter to list all objects (not just top-level) for accurate stats\n575\t\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"\", \"\", 1000)\n576\t\t\tif err != nil {\n577\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n578\t\t\t\treturn\n579\t\t\t}\n580\t\n581\t\t\tstats := EncryptionStatsResponse{\n582\t\t\t\tKeyUsage: make(map[string]int),\n583\t\t\t}\n584\t\n585\t\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n586\t\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\") {\n587\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n588\t\t\t\t}\n589\t\t\t\tstats.TotalCount++\n590\t\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n591\t\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedCount++\n592\t\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedBytes += obj.Size\n593\t\t\t\t\tkeyID := \"default\"\n594\t\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok && armorMeta.KeyID != \"\" {\n595\t\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n596\t\t\t\t\t}\n597\t\t\t\t\tstats.KeyUsage[keyID]++\n598\t\t\t\t} else {\n599\t\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextCount++\n600\t\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextBytes += obj.Size\n601\t\t\t\t}\n602\t\t\t}\n603\t\n604\t\t\tfor k := range stats.KeyUsage {\n605\t\t\t\tstats.KeyIDs = append(stats.KeyIDs, k)\n606\t\t\t}\n607\t\t\tsort.Strings(stats.KeyIDs)\n608\t\n609\t\t\tif stats.TotalCount > 0 {\n610\t\t\t\tstats.CoveragePercent = float64(stats.EncryptedCount) / float64(stats.TotalCount) * 100\n611\t\t\t}\n612\t\n613\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n614\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(stats)\n615\t\t}\n616\t}\n617\t\n618\t// ListObject represents an object in the JSON list response.\n619\ttype ListObject struct {\n620\t\tKey          string    `json:\"key\"`\n621\t\tSize         int64     `json:\"size\"`\n622\t\tLastModified string    `json:\"last_modified\"`\n623\t\tEncrypted    bool      `json:\"encrypted\"`\n624\t\tKeyID        string    `json:\"key_id,omitempty\"`\n625\t}\n626\t\n627\t// ListAPIResponse holds the JSON response for the list endpoint.\n628\ttype ListAPIResponse struct {\n629\t\tPrefix         string http.MethodGet {\n648\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n649\t\t\t\treturn\n650\t\t\t}\n651\t\n652\t\t\tprefix :=  obj.Key,\n672\t\t\t\t\tSize:         obj.Size,\n673\t\t\t\t\tLastModified: obj.LastModified.Format(time.RFC3339),\n674\t\t\t\t\tEncrypted:    obj.IsARMOREncrypted,\n675\t\t\t\t}\n676\t\t\t\tif {\n680\t\t\t\t\t\t\tlistObj.KeyID = \"default\"\n681\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n682\t\t\t\t\t}\n683\t\t\t\t}\n684\t\t\t\tresponse.Objects = append(response.Objects, listObj)\n685\t\t\t}\n686\t\n687\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n688\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)\n689\t\t}\n690\t}\n691\t\n692\t// Helper functions\n693\t\n694\tfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n695\t\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n696\t\treturn n\n697\t}\n698\t\n699\tfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n700\t\tif n < 1024 {\n701\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", n)\n702\t\t}\n703\t\tif n < 1024*1024 {\n704\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f KB\", float64(n)/1024)\n705\t\t}\n706\t\tif n < 1024*1024*1024 {\n707\t\t\treturn {\n713\t\td = d.Round(time.Second)\n714\t\th := d / time.Hour\n715\t\td -= h * time.Hour\n716\t\tm := d / time.Minute\n717\t\td -= m * time.Minute\n718\t\ts := d / time.Second\n719\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%dh %dm %ds\", h, m, s)\n720\t}\n721\t\n722\t// The HTML template for the dashboard\n723\tconst dashboardHTML = `<!DOCTYPE html>\n724\t<html lang=\"en\">\n725\t<head>\n726\t    <meta \"/\"\n\t\t\tbreadcrumbs = append(breadcrumbs, Breadcrumb{Name: part, Path: path})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Get metrics\n\tcacheHits := d.metrics.CacheHitsTotal.String()\n\tcacheMisses := float64(hits+misses) * 100\n\t\thitRate = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f%%\", rate)\n\t}\n\n\t// Build sorted key IDs list for the encryption coverage panel\n\tkeyIDs := make([]string, 0, len(keyIDSet))\n\tfor k := range keyIDSet {\n\t\tkeyIDs = append(keyIDs, k)\n\t}\n\tsort.Strings(keyIDs)\n\n\ttotalObjCount := encCount + plainCount\n\tencPct := \"0\"\n\tif totalObjCount > 0 {\n\t\tencPct = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f\", float64(encCount)/float64(totalObjCount)*100)\n\t}\n\n\tcanaryStatus, canaryCardClass := d.getCanaryStatus()\n\treturn PageData{\n\t\tBucket:           d.bucket,\n\t\tPrefix:           prefix,\n\t\tObjects:          objects,\n\t\tCacheHits:        cacheHits,\n\t\tCacheMisses:      cacheMisses,\n\t\tCacheHitRate:     hitRate,\n\t\tUptime:           formatUptime(time.Since(d.metrics.StartTime())),\n\t\tRequests:         d.metrics.RequestsTotal.String(),\n\t\tBytesUp:          formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesUploaded.String())),\n\t\tBytesDown:        formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesDownloaded.String())),\n\t\tCanaryStatus:     canaryStatus,\n\t\tCanaryCardClass:  canaryCardClass,\n\t\tBreadcrumbs:      breadcrumbs,\n\t\tEncryptedCount:   encCount,\n\t\tPlaintextCount:   plainCount,\n\t\tTotalObjectCount: totalObjCount,\n\t\tKeyIDs:           keyIDs,\n\t\tEncryptedPct:     encPct,\n\t\tRangeBytesSaved:  formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.RangeBytesSavedTotal.String())),\n\t\tKeyWrapOps:       d.metrics.KeyWrapOpsTotal.String(),\n\t\tKeyUnwrapOps:     d.metrics.KeyUnwrapOpsTotal.String(),\n\t}\n}\n\n// getCanaryStatus returns (status string, CSS card class).\n// CSS class is \"healthy\", \"unhealthy\", or \"\" for not-yet-started.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) getCanaryStatus() (string, string) {\n\t// Use Value() to get the raw string; String() returns JSON-quoted form.\n\tlastCheck := d.metrics.CanaryLastCheckTime.Value()\n\tfailures := parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.CanaryCheckFailures.String())\n\n\tif failures > 0 {\n\t\terrMsg := d.metrics.CanaryLastCheckError.Value()\n\t\tif errMsg != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Unhealthy: %s\", errMsg), \"unhealthy\"\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Unhealthy (failures: %d)\", failures), \"unhealthy\"\n\t}\n\tif lastCheck == \"\" {\n\t\treturn \"Not started\", \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Healthy (last: %s)\", lastCheck), \"healthy\"\n}\n\n// ObjectDetailHandler returns details for a specific object.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.objectDetailHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// ObjectDetailHandlerWithAuth returns the object detail handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.objectDetailHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// objectDetailHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the object detail handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) objectDetailHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tkey := r.URL.Query().Get(\"key\")\n\t\tif key == \"\" {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key parameter required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tinfo, err := d.backend.Head(ctx, d.bucket, key)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object: %v\", err), http.StatusNotFound)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Build response\n\t\tdetail := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"key\":           key,\n\t\t\t\"size\":          info.Size,\n\t\t\t\"content_type\":  info.ContentType,\n\t\t\t\"etag\":          info.ETag,\n\t\t\t\"last_modified\": info.LastModified.Format(time.RFC3339),\n\t\t\t\"is_armor\":      info.IsARMOREncrypted,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif info.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\tarmorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(info.Metadata)\n\t\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\t\tdetail[\"armor\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\t\"plaintext_size\": armorMeta.PlaintextSize,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"block_size\":     armorMeta.BlockSize,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"key_id\":         armorMeta.KeyID,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"iv\":             fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.IV),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"wrapped_dek\":    fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.WrappedDEK),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"sha256\":         armorMeta.PlaintextSHA,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(detail)\n\t}\n}\n\n// MetricsHandler returns metrics in JSON format.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.metricsHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// MetricsHandlerWithAuth returns the metrics handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.metricsHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// metricsHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the metrics handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) metricsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tm := d.metrics\n\t\tcacheHits := parseExpvarInt(m.CacheHitsTotal.String())\n\t\tcacheMisses := parseExpvarInt(m.CacheMissesTotal.String())\n\t\tvar cacheHitRatePct float64\n\t\tif cacheHits+cacheMisses > 0 {\n\t\t\tcacheHitRatePct = float64(cacheHits) / float64(cacheHits+cacheMisses) * 100\n\t\t}\n\t\tdata := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"requests_total\":        parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"requests_in_flight\":    parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsInFlight.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_uploaded\":        parseExpvarInt(m.BytesUploaded.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_downloaded\":      parseExpvarInt(m.BytesDownloaded.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_fetched_from_b2\": parseExpvarInt(m.BytesFetchedFromB2.String()),\n\t\t\t\"range_reads_total\":     parseExpvarInt(m.RangeReadsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"range_bytes_saved\":     parseExpvarInt(m.RangeBytesSavedTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"cache_hits\":            cacheHits,\n\t\t\t\"cache_misses\":          cacheMisses,\n\t\t\t\"cache_hit_rate_pct\":    cacheHitRatePct,\n\t\t\t\"key_wrap_ops\":          parseExpvarInt(m.KeyWrapOpsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"key_unwrap_ops\":        parseExpvarInt(m.KeyUnwrapOpsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"canary_checks\":         parseExpvarInt(m.CanaryChecksTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"canary_failures\":       parseExpvarInt(m.CanaryCheckFailures.String()),\n\t\t\t\"active_multipart\":      parseExpvarInt(m.ActiveMultipartUploads.String()),\n\t\t\t\"provenance_entries\":    parseExpvarInt(m.ProvenanceEntriesTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"uptime_seconds\":        time.Since(m.StartTime()).Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\"uptime_formatted\":      formatUptime(time.Since(m.StartTime())),\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(data)\n\t}\n}\n\n// KeyRotateHandler handles key rotation requests.\n// It generates a new MEK and calls the admin API to perform rotation.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandler(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL)\n}\n\n// KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth handles key rotation requests with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL))\n}\n\n// keyRotateHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the key rotation handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n\t\tif _, err := rand.Read(newMEK); err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate new MEK: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Call the admin API's rotate endpoint\n\t\trotateURL := adminURL\n\t\tif rotateURL == \"\" {\n\t\t\trotateURL = \"http://127.0.0.1:9001/admin/key/rotate\"\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Send the new MEK as hex-encoded string\n\t\tmekHex := hex.EncodeToString(newMEK)\n\t\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(r.Context(), http.MethodPost, rotateURL, strings.NewReader(mekHex))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to create request: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\treq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\")\n\n\t\tresp, err := adminClient.Do(req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to call admin API: %v\", err), http.StatusBadGateway)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n\n\t\t// Copy response headers and body\n\t\tfor k, v := range resp.Header {\n\t\t\tw.Header()[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(resp.StatusCode)\n\t\tio.Copy(w, resp.Body)\n\t}\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsResponse holds encryption statistics for a bucket listing.\ntype EncryptionStatsResponse struct {\n\tEncryptedCount  int            `json:\"encrypted_count\"`\n\tPlaintextCount  int            `json:\"plaintext_count\"`\n\tTotalCount      int            `json:\"total_count\"`\n\tEncryptedBytes  int64          `json:\"encrypted_bytes\"`\n\tPlaintextBytes  int64          `json:\"plaintext_bytes\"`\n\tKeyIDs          []string       `json:\"key_ids\"`\n\tKeyUsage        map[string]int `json:\"key_usage\"`\n\tCoveragePercent float64        `json:\"coverage_percent\"`\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsHandler returns encryption statistics for the bucket.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth returns the encryption stats handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl())\n}\n\nfunc (d *Dashboard) encryptionStatsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\t// Use no delimiter to list all objects (not just top-level) for accurate stats\n\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"\", \"\", 1000)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tstats := EncryptionStatsResponse{\n\t\t\tKeyUsage: make(map[string]int),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\") {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tstats.TotalCount++\n\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedCount++\n\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedBytes += obj.Size\n\t\t\t\tkeyID := \"default\"\n\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok && armorMeta.KeyID != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tstats.KeyUsage[keyID]++\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextCount++\n\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextBytes += obj.Size\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor k := range stats.KeyUsage {\n\t\t\tstats.KeyIDs = append(stats.KeyIDs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Strings(stats.KeyIDs)\n\n\t\tif stats.TotalCount > 0 {\n\t\t\tstats.CoveragePercent = float64(stats.EncryptedCount) / float64(stats.TotalCount) * 100\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(stats)\n\t}\n}\n\n// ListObject represents an object in the JSON list response.\ntype ListObject struct {\n\tKey          string    `json:\"key\"`\n\tSize         int64     `json:\"size\"`\n\tLastModified string    `json:\"last_modified\"`\n\tEncrypted    bool      `json:\"encrypted\"`\n\tKeyID        string    `json:\"key_id,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// ListAPIResponse holds the JSON response for the list endpoint.\ntype ListAPIResponse struct {\n\tPrefix         string       `json:\"prefix\"`\n\tObjects        []ListObject `json:\"objects\"`\n\tCommonPrefixes []string     `json:\"common_prefixes\"`\n}\n\n// ListAPIHandler returns the JSON list handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ListAPIHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.listAPIHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// ListAPIHandlerWithAuth returns the JSON list handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ListAPIHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.listAPIHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// listAPIHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the JSON list handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) listAPIHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"/\", \"\", 1000)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresponse := ListAPIResponse{\n\t\t\tPrefix:         prefix,\n\t\t\tObjects:        make([]ListObject, 0, len(result.Objects)),\n\t\t\tCommonPrefixes: result.CommonPrefixes,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\tlistObj := ListObject{\n\t\t\t\tKey:          obj.Key,\n\t\t\t\tSize:         obj.Size,\n\t\t\t\tLastModified: obj.LastModified.Format(time.RFC3339),\n\t\t\t\tEncrypted:    obj.IsARMOREncrypted,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tlistObj.KeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n\t\t\t\t\tif listObj.KeyID == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tlistObj.KeyID = \"default\"\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tresponse.Objects = append(response.Objects, listObj)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Helper functions\n\nfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n\treturn n\n}\n\nfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n\tif n < 1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", n)\n\t}\n\tif n < 1024*1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f KB\", float64(n)/1024)\n\t}\n\tif n < 1024*1024*1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f MB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024))\n\t}\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f GB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024*1024))\n}\n\nfunc formatUptime(d time.Duration) string {\n\td = d.Round(time.Second)\n\th := d / time.Hour\n\td -= h * time.Hour\n\tm := d / time.Minute\n\td -= m * time.Minute\n\ts := d / time.Second\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%dh %dm %ds\", h, m, s)\n}\n\n// The httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\t// No auth header - should fail\n\tif auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to fail without credentials\")\n\t}\n\tif rec.Code != token\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/dashboard\", nil)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", \"Bearer my-secret-token\")\n\trec := httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\tif !auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to succeed with valid token\")\n\t}\n\t// On success, Authenticate returns true and doesn't write to response\n\tif rec.Code != 0 && rec.Code != http.StatusOK {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected no error status on success, got %d\", rec.Code)\n\t}\n\n\t// Invalid token\n\treq = httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/dashboard\", nil)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", \"Bearer wrong-token\")\n\trec = httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\tif auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to fail with invalid token\")\n\t}\n\tif rec.Code != http.StatusUnauthorized {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected status 401 on invalid token, got %d\", rec.Code)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Test authentication middleware with no auth 300,\n\t\tIsARMOREncrypted: true,\n\t\tLastModified:     time.Now(),\n\t\tMetadata: map[string]string{\n\t\t\t\"x-amz-meta-armor-version\":        \"1\",\n\t\t\t\"x-amz-meta-armor-block-size\":     \"65536\",\n\t\t\t\"x-amz-meta-armor-plaintext-size\": \"300\",\n\t\t\t\"x-amz-meta-armor-key-id\":         \"keyB\",\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\tmb.objects[\"plain.txt\"] = &backend.ObjectInfo{\n\t\tKey:          \"plain.txt\",\n\t\tSize:         100,\n\t\tLastModified: time.Now(),\n\t}\n\n\tm := metrics.NewMetrics()\n\td := New(mb, \"test-bucket\", m)\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, rec.Code)\n\t}\n\n\tvar stats EncryptionStatsResponse\n\tif err := json.NewDecoder(rec.Body).Decode(&stats); err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to decode response: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tif stats.EncryptedCount != 2 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected 2 encrypted objects, got %d\", stats.EncryptedCount)\n\t}\n\tif stats.PlaintextCount != 1 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected 1 plaintext object, got %d\",
